---
about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> Population decoding is
  a powerful way to analyze neural data - from single cell recordings, fMRI, MEG,
  EEG, etc - to understand the information it contains and how it is encoded. Case
  study of visual object recognition in primate visual cortex.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Ethan Meyers</p>
course_id: res-9-003-brains-minds-and-machines-summer-course-summer-2015

  <span m='3148430'>to</span> <span m='3148550'>do</span> <span m='3148700'>that</span>
  <span m='3149460'>invariance</span> <span m='3150950'>or</span> <span m='3151340'>abstract</span>
  <span m='3151850'>analysis.</span> <span m='3152600'>Or</span> <span m='3152780'>you</span>
  <span m='3152930'>can</span> <span m='3153500'>do</span> <span m='3153620'>things</span>
  <span m='3153890'>like,</span> <span m='3154130'>I</span> <span m='3154190'>guess,</span>
  <span m='3154430'>change</span> <span m='3154760'>the</span> <span m='3154820'>different</span>
  <span m='3155060'>binning</span> <span m='3155360'>schemes</span> <span m='3155870'>within</span>
  <span m='3156170'>that</span> <span m='3157730'>piece</span> <span m='3157940'>of</span>
  <span m='3158030'>code.</span> </p><p><span m='3158410'>So</span> <span m='3158500'>that's</span>
  <span m='3158660'>one</span> <span m='3158810'>component</span> <span m='3159170'>you
  can</span> <span m='3159290'>swap</span> <span m='3159530'>in</span> <span m='3159620'>and</span>
  <span m='3159710'>out.</span> <span m='3160310'>Another</span> <span m='3160580'>one</span>
  <span m='3160880'>are</span> <span m='3160970'>these</span> <span m='3161180'>preprocessors.</span>
